  <script>

		document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

			const wrapper = document.getElementById('toggle-account-menu');

			const wrapperMobile = document.getElementById('toggle-account-menu-mobile');

			if (wrapperMobile) {

				wrapperMobile.addEventListener('click', () => {

					const menuMobile = document.getElementById('header-account-menu-mobile');

					if (menuMobile.classList.contains('hidden')) {

						menuMobile.classList.remove('hidden');

						menuMobile.classList.add('flex');

					} else {

						menuMobile.classList.add('hidden');

						menuMobile.classList.remove('flex');

					}

				});

			}

			if (!wrapper) return;

			const menu = document.getElementById('header-account-menu');

			let hideTimeout;



			wrapper.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {

				clearTimeout(hideTimeout);

				menu.classList.remove('hidden');

				menu.classList.add('flex');

			});



			wrapper.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {

				hideTimeout = setTimeout(() => {

					menu.classList.add('hidden');

					menu.classList.remove('flex');

				}, 150); // slight delay allows smooth transition to the menu

			});



			// Prevent menu from hiding if hovering directly into it

			menu.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {

				clearTimeout(hideTimeout);

			});



			menu.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {

				hideTimeout = setTimeout(() => {

					menu.classList.add('hidden');

					menu.classList.remove('flex');

				}, 150);

			});

		});

	</script>

           <li>El costo de envío a cualquier destino nacional (excepto para los lugares indicados a continuación) es gratuito para compras superiores a $100.000 COP (cien mil pesos). Para compras inferiores a este valor, el costo de envío es de $9.900 COP (nueve mil novecientos pesos).</li>

           <li>Para los destinos de San Andrés y Providencia, Santa Catalina, Chocó, Vichada, Cauca, Guainía, Meta, Amazonas y Vaupés, el costo de envío deberá ser cotizado previamente, antes de realizar el pago. Ten en cuenta que el valor del envío puede variar según el tipo de producto, peso y volumen del paquete, en todo caso el mismo tendrá un valor mínimo de $50.000 COP (cincuenta mil pesos) por cada artículo.</li>

           <li>Para compras internacionales, el costo de envío será asumido por el cliente y dependerá del destino y el volumen del paquete.</li>

     <p>Esta tabla de medidas es aproximada y le ayudará a encontrar su talla de zapatos.</p>

  <script>



	document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

		var accordions = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-header');



		accordions.forEach(function (header) {

			header.addEventListener('click', function () {

				var content = this.nextElementSibling;

				console.log(content);

				var icon = this.querySelector('.icono');

				this.classList.toggle('!border-b-0');

				icon.classList.toggle('after:-rotate-90');





				// Toggle the 'expanded' class to animate max-height

				if (content.classList.contains('expanded')) {

					content.classList.remove('expanded');

				} else {

					content.classList.add('expanded');

				}

			});

		});

	});



	const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {

		const stars = document.querySelectorAll('.yotpo-sr-bottom-line-summary');



		if (stars.length) {

			observer.disconnect(); // Stop observing once elements are found



			stars.forEach(function (star) {

				star.addEventListener('click', function () {

					console.log('click');

					const content = document.getElementById('reviews-content');

					const reviewsHeader = document.getElementById('reviews-header');

					const icon = reviewsHeader.querySelector('.icono');



					console.log(content);

					console.log(reviewsHeader);

					console.log(icon);





					if (reviewsHeader && icon && content) {

						reviewsHeader.classList.add('!border-b-0');

						icon.classList.add('after:-rotate-90');

						content.classList.add('expanded');

					}

				});

			});

		}

	});



	// Observe the document body for child node changes

	observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });









</script>

  <script>

	jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {

		// Listen for the 'found_variation' event triggered by WooCommerce

		$('form.variations_form').on('found_variation', function (event, variation) {

			// Access the value of `attribute_pa_talla`

			const tallaValue = variation.attributes.attribute_pa_talla;

			const ref = $('#ref').text();

			const thumbUrl = $('#hidden-thumb').data('thumb');

			console.log(thumbUrl)

			const date = new Date().toLocaleString('es-MX', {

				day: '2-digit',

				month: '2-digit',

				year: 'numeric',

				hour: '2-digit',

				minute: '2-digit',

				second: '2-digit',

				hour12: false

			}).replace(',', '')

			const productName = $('input[name="hidden-1"]').val();



			// Log the value to the console (for debugging)

			console.log('Selected Talla:', tallaValue);



			// Target the Forminator select field using a flexible selector

			const selectField = $('input[name="text-3"]');

			const refField = $('input[name="text-2"]');

			const imageField = $('input[name="text-4"]');

			refField.val(ref);

			imageField.val(thumbUrl);

			refField.attr('readonly', true);

			selectField.attr('readonly', true);



			const entryTitle = `${productName} - ${ref} - ${date}`;







			$('input[name="postdata-1-post-title"]').val(entryTitle);



			if (selectField.length) {

				selectField.val(tallaValue).trigger('change'); // Set the value and trigger change event

			} else {

				console.error('Forminator select field not found!');

			}



			// Show the modal if the selected variation is out of stock

			if (!variation.is_in_stock) {

				$('#out-of-stock-modal').show();

				$('body').addClass('overflow-hidden'); // Enable scrolling



			}

		});



		// Close the modal when the close button is clicked

		$('#close-modal').on('click', function () {

			$('#out-of-stock-modal').hide();

			$('body').removeClass('overflow-hidden'); // Enable scrolling

		});



		jQuery(document).on('forminator:form:submit:success', function (event) {

			// Close the modal using jQuery

			setTimeout(() => {

				$('#out-of-stock-modal').hide();

				$('body').removeClass('overflow-hidden'); // Enable scrolling

			}, 3000);

		});

	});

</script>

  <script>

	jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {

		function triggerCheckoutUpdate() {

			$('body').trigger('update_checkout');

			console.log("Checkout updated");

		}



		function isShippingDifferent() {

			return $('#ship-to-different-address input').is(':checked');

		}



		// Listen for changes in billing fields but only update if shipping is NOT different

		$('form.checkout, form.woocommerce-shipping-calculator').on('change',

			'select#billing_country, select#billing_state, select#billing_city',

			function () {

				if (!isShippingDifferent()) {

					triggerCheckoutUpdate();

				}

			}

		);



		// Always update checkout when shipping fields change

		$('form.checkout, form.woocommerce-shipping-calculator').on('change',

			'select#shipping_country, select#shipping_state, select#shipping_city, ' +

			'select#select2-shipping_country-container, select#select2-shipping_state-container, select#select2-shipping_city-container',

			triggerCheckoutUpdate

		);



		// When "Ship to a different address?" checkbox is toggled, update checkout

		$('#ship-to-different-address input').on('change', function () {

			triggerCheckoutUpdate();

		});

	});

</script>

  <script>

	(function ($) {

		$.fn.inputFilter = function (inputFilter) {

			return this.on(

				"input keydown keyup mousedown mouseup select contextmenu drop",

				function () {

					console.log("key");

					if (inputFilter(this.value)) {

						this.oldValue = this.value;

						this.oldSelectionStart = this.selectionStart;

						this.oldSelectionEnd = this.selectionEnd;

					} else if (this.hasOwnProperty("oldValue")) {

						this.value = this.oldValue;

						this.setSelectionRange(this.oldSelectionStart, this.oldSelectionEnd);

					} else {

						this.value = "";

					}

				}

			);

		};

	})(jQuery);



	jQuery(window).on("load", function () {

		jQuery("#username, #account_username, #reg_username, #billing_user_login, #nf-field-12").inputFilter(

			function (value) {

				return /^\d*$/.test(value); // Allow digits only, using a RegExp

			}

		);

	});



</script>
